\documentclass[]{ximera}

\begin{document}
\input{JasonSageMacros}
\renewcommand{\latexProblemContent}[1]{#1}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%%\tagged{Cat@One, Cat@Two, Cat@Three, Cat@Four, Cat@Five, Ans@MultiAns, Type@Concept, Topic@Limit, Sub@Continuity, Sub@Disc_Jump, Sub@Piecewise}{
\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\

\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=$\answer{None} \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



\begin{sagesilent}
a = Integer(randint(-3,3))
b = NonZeroInt(a+2,a+5)

c = RandInt(-5,5)
c2 = RandInt(-5,5)
c3 = RandInt(-5,5)

func1=[x-c, c-x, (x-c)^2, expand((x-c)*(x-c2))]
func2=[x, x^2-c3*x, x^2+c3*x, (x-c3)^2]

p1 = RandInt(0,3)
p2 = RandInt(0,3)
p3 = RandInt(0,3)

f1 = func1[p1]
F2 = func2[p2]
F3 = func2[p3]

A = f1(a) - F3(a) + 1
f3 = F3 + A
B = f1(b)- F2(b)
f2 = F2 + B

\end{sagesilent}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
\sage{f3} & , & x\leq \sage{a}\\
\sage{f1} & , & \sage{a}<x\leq\sage{b}\\
\sage{f2} & , & x>\sage{b}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{2311_Concept_Limit_0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{\sage{a}}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}
